\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
C\+M\+S\+IS Cortex-\/\+M4 Peripheral Access Layer Header File for for the Active Semiconductor P\+A\+C55\+XX Device Family. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Copyright (C) 2017-\/2019, Qorvo, Inc.
\end{DoxyNote}
T\+H\+IS S\+O\+F\+T\+W\+A\+RE IS S\+U\+B\+J\+E\+CT TO A S\+O\+U\+R\+CE C\+O\+DE L\+I\+C\+E\+N\+SE A\+G\+R\+E\+E\+M\+E\+NT W\+H\+I\+CH P\+R\+O\+V\+I\+D\+ES, A\+M\+O\+NG O\+T\+H\+ER T\+H\+I\+N\+GS\+: (i) T\+H\+AT IT C\+AN BE U\+S\+ED O\+N\+LY TO A\+D\+A\+PT T\+HE L\+I\+C\+E\+N\+S\+EE\textquotesingle{}S A\+P\+P\+L\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON TO P\+AC P\+R\+O\+C\+E\+S\+S\+O\+RS S\+U\+P\+P\+L\+I\+ED BY Q\+O\+R\+VO, I\+NC.; (ii) T\+H\+AT IT IS P\+R\+O\+V\+I\+D\+ED \char`\"{}\+A\+S I\+S\char`\"{} W\+I\+T\+H\+O\+UT W\+A\+R\+R\+A\+N\+TY; (iii) T\+H\+AT Q\+O\+R\+VO, I\+NC. IS N\+OT L\+I\+A\+B\+LE F\+OR A\+NY I\+N\+D\+I\+R\+E\+CT D\+A\+M\+A\+G\+ES OR F\+OR D\+I\+R\+E\+CT D\+A\+M\+A\+G\+ES E\+X\+C\+E\+E\+D\+I\+NG US\$1,500; A\+ND (iv) T\+H\+AT IT C\+AN BE D\+I\+S\+C\+L\+O\+S\+ED TO A\+ND U\+S\+ED O\+N\+LY BY C\+E\+R\+T\+A\+IN A\+U\+T\+H\+O\+R\+I\+Z\+ED P\+E\+R\+S\+O\+NS.
